***verdieping.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdieping.html>verdieping</a> (2209)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verdiepinge</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdiepen.html>verdiepen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdieping.html>verdieping</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdiepingen.html>verdiepingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdieping.html>verdiepinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>deepening</li>
<li>floor, storey</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In the Dutch-speaking countries, the first floor <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the floor one level above ground level. The ground floor <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> called <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begane.html>begane</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grond.html>grond</a></i>. Until the seventeenth century <i><a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdieping.html>verdieping</a></i> could mean both âground floorâ and âfirst floorâ.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">floor</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:etage.html>etage</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:verdieping.html>verdieping</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dieper.html>dieper</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bepaalde.html>bepaalde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:diepte.html>diepte</a></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdoemen.html>verdoemen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fradÅmijanÄ</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doem.html>doem</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdoemenis.html>verdoemenis</a> (12654)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verdoemenisse</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdoemen.html>verdoemen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-nis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdoemenis.html>verdoemenis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verdoemenis.html>verdoemenissen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> damnation, perdition</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> condemnation, guilty verdict</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:verdoemenis.html>verdoemenis</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
